    15 2. Auto-sync new users to profiles on INSERT.
    16    - Set search_path = public to resolve types correctly.
    17    - The following template has been validated as a best practice and is compatible with any business requirements. Only the custom registration fields to be synchronized in handle_new_user may be modified. No other changes are allowed, and no additional trigger logic may be added to the auth table.
    18 Template:
    19 ```sql
    20 CREATE TYPE public.user_role AS ENUM ('user', 'admin');
    21 
    22 CREATE FUNCTION handle_new_user()
    23 RETURNS trigger
    24 LANGUAGE plpgsql
    25 SECURITY DEFINER SET search_path = public
    26 AS $$
    27 BEGIN
    28 -- Insert a profile synced with fields collected at signup.
    29 INSERT INTO public.profiles (id, email, phone, role)
    30 VALUES (
    31   NEW.id,
    32   NEW.email,
    33   NEW.phone,
    34   'user'::public.user_role
    35 );
    36 RETURN NEW;
    37 END;
    38 $$;
    39 
    40 -- Do not add any additional triggers to the auth table.
    41 CREATE TRIGGER on_auth_user_created
    42   AFTER INSERT ON auth.users
    43   FOR EACH ROW
    44   EXECUTE FUNCTION handle_new_user();
    45 ```
    46 3. AuthContext / RouteGuard:
    47     - Always add AuthProvider in @/App.tsx so all pages can access login state (e.g. navbar login/logout).
    48     - RouteGuard is optional: only add it when authentication is required for most routes.
    49       - If the app pattern is "only admin needs login, other routes are public", do NOT add RouteGuard. Its default-block-all interception (whitelist-only) will break the app for regular users.
    50       - When RouteGuard IS needed: review @/contexts/AuthContext.tsx and @/components/common/RouteGuard.tsx, do not create new files. Check PUBLIC_ROUTES and add RouteGuard in @/App.tsx.
    51 4. Show login status and login/logout in navbar(add header in app.tsx); if without a navbar, add a login/logout button, login status on the home page.
    52 5. After a successful login, the user must be redirected to a non-login page.
    53 6. If roles/admin needed:
    54    - AI must create one example admin account with a randomly generated, strong password (16+ chars, mixed case + digits + symbols). Never use simple passwords unless the user explicitly specifies one. Output the credentials in the finish summary.
    55    - **TIMING: Execute the three steps below immediately after the auth migration runs — do NOT defer to the end of the task. Context compression may cause this step to be skipped if left until later.**
    56    - Account creation flow (three-step, fully automated via script):
    57      1. Register using the anon key: call `supabase.auth.signUp({ email, password })` with the normal client (anon key). This triggers `handle_new_user` to insert the profiles row with `role='user'`.
    58      2. If email verification is enabled, use the `supabase_execute_sql` tool to bypass it. Skip this step if verification is already disabled.
    59      3. Use the `supabase_execute_sql` tool to promote the user to admin in the profiles table. Do NOT ask the user to change the role manually.
    60      Example script pattern:
    61      ```javascript
    62      // Step 1: Register with anon key
    63      const { data: authData } = await supabase.auth.signUp({ email: `${username}@miaoda.com`, password });
    64      ```
    65      Step 2: If verification is enabled, use the `supabase_execute_sql` tool to bypass it:
    66      ```sql
    67      -- username+password: confirm by email
    68      UPDATE auth.users SET email_confirmed_at = NOW(), confirmed_at = NOW() WHERE email = '<username>@miaoda.com';
    69 
    70      -- phone+OTP: confirm by phone
    71      UPDATE auth.users SET phone_confirmed_at = NOW(), confirmed_at = NOW() WHERE phone = '<phone>';
    72      ```
    73      Step 3: Use the `supabase_execute_sql` tool to promote the user to admin (query by the identifier used at signup — email for username+password, phone for phone+OTP, email for email+password):
    74      ```sql
    75      -- username+password: query by email (username@miaoda.com)
    76      UPDATE public.profiles SET role = 'admin' WHERE email = '<username>@miaoda.com';
    77 
    78      -- phone+OTP: query by phone
    79      UPDATE public.profiles SET role = 'admin' WHERE phone = '<phone>';
    80 
    81      -- email+password: query by email
    82      UPDATE public.profiles SET role = 'admin' WHERE email = '<email>';
    83      ```
    84    - The script must be executed automatically as part of the setup; log the resulting credentials (username + password) to the console.
    85    - Admin sees Admin entry in navbar.
    86    - Admin page: manage user roles (edit others).
    87    - profiles permissions:
    88      1. Create helper `get_user_role` (SECURITY DEFINER) to prevent infinite recursion detected in policy for relation "profiles"
    89      2. Admins have full access
    90      3. Users can view own data
    91      4. Users can edit own data except `role`
    92      5. Use `public_profiles` view for shareable info
    93      Here is an example:
    94 ```sql
    95 CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION get_user_role(uid uuid)
    96 RETURNS user_role
    97 LANGUAGE sql
    98 SECURITY DEFINER
    99 SET search_path = public
   100 AS $$
   101   SELECT role FROM profiles WHERE id = uid;
   102 $$;
   103 
   104 -- Profiles policies
   105 CREATE POLICY "Admins have full access to profiles" ON profiles
   106   FOR ALL TO authenticated USING (get_user_role(auth.uid()) = 'admin'::user_role);
   107 
   108 CREATE POLICY "Users can view their own profile" ON profiles
   109   FOR SELECT TO authenticated USING (auth.uid() = id);
   110 
   111 CREATE POLICY "Users can update their own profile" ON profiles
   112   FOR UPDATE TO authenticated USING (auth.uid() = id)
   113   WITH CHECK (role IS NOT DISTINCT FROM get_user_role(auth.uid()));
   114 
   115 CREATE VIEW public_profiles AS
   116   SELECT id, role FROM profiles;
   117 ```
   118 
   119 7. Anonymous login (if needed):
   120    - On first visit, generate a UUID v4 as the anonymous credential ID and persist it in localStorage under the key `anon_credential_id`. This is NOT the Supabase auth.uid — it is an app-level identifier.
   121    - Create a table `anon_credential_map (credential_id uuid PRIMARY KEY, auth_uid uuid REFERENCES profiles(id))` to store the mapping. RLS: only the Edge Function's service-role key may read/write this table.
   122    - Create a Supabase Edge Function `anon-auth` that:
   123      1. Accepts `{ credential_id: string }` in the request body.
   124      2. Queries `anon_credential_map` for the given credential_id.
   125      3. If found: calls `supabaseAdmin.auth.admin.generateLink({ type: 'magiclink', email })` to generate a token for the existing user.
   126      4. If not found: first calls `supabaseAdmin.auth.admin.createUser({ email: 'anon_<credential_id>@miaoda.com', password: <random strong password>, email_confirm: true })` to register the user, inserts the credential_id → auth.uid row into `anon_credential_map`, then calls `generateLink` to generate a token.
   127      5. Returns `{ hashed_token }` (from `data.properties.hashed_token`) to the client.
   128    - On the client, call `supabase.auth.verifyOtp({ token_hash: hashed_token, type: 'magiclink' })` to activate the session.
   129    - The Edge Function must use the service-role key (server-side only, never exposed to the client).
   130    - The credential_id must never be sent to any third party and must only be used for this Edge Function call.
   131    - Note: the `on_auth_user_created` trigger will fire for anonymous users too; ensure the profiles table allows null email and phone.
   132 
   133 
   134 Recommended:
   135 1. If no method specified, use username + password.
   136 2. Login must check `supabase_verification`; show phone/email verification UI if enabled.

   138 
   139 
   140 Tech limits:
   141 1. Unregistered users can't set roles; register first via signUp, then use the `supabase_execute_sql` tool to update role.
   142 2. Single account system; multi-device handled by roles.
   143 3. Password changes/add accounts via Edge Functions (do not use trigger for auth→profiles).
   144 4. Do not insert into profiles directly; only trigger sync adds rows.

   158 6. Any other manual steps the user must perform (Supabase Dashboard changes, environment variable settings, role updates, etc.).
   159 
   160 Auth notes:
   161 1. Username + password:
   162   - simulate email/password with @miaoda.com
   163   - use `supabase_verification` tool to disable email verification
   164   - Only letters, digits, and _ are allowed in usernames.
   165 2. Google SSO:
   166 ```
   167 const { data, error } = await client.auth.signInWithSSO({
   168   domain: 'miaoda-gg.com',
   169   options: { redirectTo: window.location.origin },
   170 });
   171 window.open(data.url, '_self');
   172 ```
   173 Do not use OAuth.
   174 3. Phone OTP:
   175    - Use `signInWithOtp()` to send OTP, `verifyOtp()` to login. No other SMS APIs.
   176 ```tsx
   177 // Step 1: Send OTP
   178 const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithOtp({
   179   phone: "+86" + phoneNumber,
   180 });
   181 
   182 // Step 2: Verify OTP
   183 const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.verifyOtp({
   184   phone: "+86" + phoneNumber,
   185   token: otpCode,
   186   type: "sms",
   187 });
   188 ```
   189    - **CRITICAL — `sms-verification` plugin conflict**: The project scaffold may include a `sms-verification` plugin or component (e.g. `SmsVerification`, `useSmsCode`, `sendSmsCode`). This plugin manages its own SMS state and will conflict with Supabase OTP flow — both systems attempt to control the same verification lifecycle, causing double-sends, state desync, or silent failures.
   190      - **NEVER** wire the `sms-verification` plugin into the phone login flow.
   191      - If such a component exists in the codebase, do NOT import or call it from the login/register page. Build the OTP UI directly using only `supabase.auth.signInWithOtp()` and `supabase.auth.verifyOtp()`.
   192 4. Phone + password (verification ON): Use signUp(phone) to send OTP (Password required), verifyOtp() to register.
   193 5. Email + password (verification ON): pass emailRedirectTo to signup (default window.location.origin).

     1 import React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState, useCallback } from 'react';
     2 import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     3 import { AuthContextType, Profile, RegisterData } from '@/types/types';
     4 import { toast } from 'sonner';
     5 import { User } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
     6 
     7 const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | undefined>(undefined);
     8 
     9 /** 从 auth.User 元数据中构建兜底 profile，避免 fetchProfile 失败时用户卡在登录页 */
    10 function buildFallbackProfile(authUser: User): Profile {
    11   const meta = authUser.user_metadata ?? {};
    12   const email = authUser.email ?? '';
    13   const username = meta.username ?? email.split('@')[0] ?? authUser.id;
    14   return {
    15     id: authUser.id,
    16     username,
    17     email,
    18     display_name: meta.display_name ?? username,
    19     user_type: meta.user_type ?? 'jobseeker',
    20     role: meta.role ?? 'user',
    21     avatar_url: meta.avatar_url ?? null,
    22     bio: null,
    23     location: null,
    24     website: null,
    25     phone: null,
    26     created_at: authUser.created_at ?? new Date().toISOString(),
    27     updated_at: authUser.updated_at ?? new Date().toISOString(),
    28   } as unknown as Profile;
    29 }
    30 
    31 export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
    32   const [user, setUser] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
    33   const [session, setSession] = useState<unknown>(null);
    34   const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
    35 
    36   const fetchProfile = useCallback(async (userId: string) => {
    37     const { data, error } = await supabase
    38       .from('profiles')
    39       .select('*')
    40       .eq('id', userId)
    41       .maybeSingle();
    42     if (error) {
    43       console.error('获取用户信息失败:', error);
    44       return null;
    45     }
    46     return data as Profile | null;
    47   }, []);
    48 
    49   const refreshProfile = useCallback(async () => {
    50     const { data: { session: currentSession } } = await supabase.auth.getSession();
    51     if (currentSession?.user) {
    52       const profile = await fetchProfile(currentSession.user.id);
    53       setUser(profile);
    54     }
    55   }, [fetchProfile]);
    56 
    57   useEffect(() => {
    58     // 初始化获取session
    59     supabase.auth.getSession().then(({ data: { session: s } }) => {
    60       setSession(s);
    61       if (s?.user) {
    62         fetchProfile(s.user.id).then(profile => {
    63           setUser(profile ?? buildFallbackProfile(s.user!));
    64           setIsLoading(false);
    65         });
    66       } else {
    67         setIsLoading(false);
    68       }
    69     });
    70 
    71     // 监听auth状态变化（回调必须是同步的，异步 await 会阻塞 signInWithPassword 返回）
    72     const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((event, s) => {
    73       setSession(s);
    74       if (s?.user) {
    75         // 用 .then() 异步更新 profile，不阻塞 auth 回调
    76         fetchProfile(s.user.id).then(profile => {
    77           setUser(profile ?? buildFallbackProfile(s.user!));
    78         });
    79       } else {
    80         setUser(null);
    81       }
    82       if (event === 'SIGNED_IN') {
    83         setIsLoading(false);
    84       }
    85     });
    86 
    87     return () => subscription.unsubscribe();
    88   }, [fetchProfile]);
    89 
    90   const login = async (username: string, password: string) => {
    91     const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
    92     const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
    93     if (error) {
    94       toast.error('登录失败：' + (error.message.includes('Invalid') ? '用户名或密码错误' : error.message));
    95       throw error;
    96     }
    97     toast.success('登录成功');
    98   };
    99 
   100   const register = async (data: RegisterData) => {
   101     const email = `${data.username}@miaoda.com`;
   102     const { data: authData, error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
   103       email,
   104       password: data.password,
   105       options: {
   106         data: {
   107           username: data.username,
   108           display_name: data.display_name,
   109           user_type: data.user_type,
   110         }
   111       }
   112     });
   113     if (error) {
   114       if (error.message.includes('already registered') || error.message.includes('unique')) {
   115         toast.error('注册失败：用户名已存在');
   116       } else {
   117         toast.error('注册失败：' + error.message);
   118       }
   119       throw error;
   120     }
   121 
   122     // 如果是企业用户，创建企业信息
   123     if (data.user_type === 'enterprise' && data.company_name && authData.user) {
   124       await supabase.from('enterprise_profiles').insert({
   125         profile_id: authData.user.id,
   126         company_name: data.company_name,
   127       });
   128     }
   129 
   130     toast.success('注册成功，欢迎加入！');
   131   };
   132 
   133   const logout = async () => {
   134     await supabase.auth.signOut();
   135     setUser(null);
   136     setSession(null);
   137     toast.success('已退出登录');
   138   };
   139 
   140   const value: AuthContextType = {
   141     user,
   142     session,
   143     isLoading,
   144     isAuthenticated: !!user,
   145     login,
   146     register,
   147     logout,
   148     refreshProfile,
   149   };
   150 
   151   return <AuthContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</AuthContext.Provider>;
   152 }
   153 
   154 export function useAuth() {
   155   const context = useContext(AuthContext);
   156   if (!context) {
   157     throw new Error('useAuth 必须在 AuthProvider 内部使用');
   158   }
   159   return context;
   160 }

The auth flow uses `username@miaoda.com` as email (e.g., user enters "dd", it becomes "dd@miaoda.com")\n2. The existing users in auth.users all have emails like "dd@miaoda.com", "ss@miaoda.com" etc.\n3. Email verification is already enabled (email_confirmed_at is set for existing users)\n\nThe error "Invalid login credentials" from Supabase typically means:\n1. The email/password combination doesn\'t match\n2. The user doesn\'t exist\n3. Email verification is required but not completed\n\nI just disabled email verification, which should help for new registrations. But existing users already have email_confirmed_at set, so they should be fine.\n\nThe real issue could be: When a user registers via `signUp()`, if email verification is ENABLED at the time of registration, Supabase doesn\'t auto-confirm the account. The user needs to click an email link first. But looking at the existing users, they all have `email_confirmed_at` set which means they were confirmed.\n\nWait - there could be another issue. When `signUp` is called and the email is already registered, Supabase returns a fake "success" response (to prevent email enumeration) but doesn\'t actually create a new account. So if the user tries to register with an existing username, they get no error, then try to login and get "Invalid login credentials" because the password they just set wasn\'t saved.\n\nBut the main fix needed: I\'ve already disabled email verification. Let me also check if there\'s an issue with the registration flow itself.\n\nLooking at the register function in AuthContext.tsx:\n1. It calls `signUp` with the email and password\n2. If email verification was enabled during signup, Supabase wouldn\'t auto-confirm the account\n3. Then `login` is called immediately after, which would fail with "Invalid login credentials" because the email hasn\'t been confirmed\n\nThe fix: \n1. I already disabled email verification via `supabase_verification` tool\n2. This means new signups will be auto-confirmed\n\nBut what about users who registered WHEN verification was enabled? Their accounts may be in a limbo state - created but not confirmed. ```
New String: ```
  const register = async (data: RegisterData) => {
    const email = `${data.username}@miaoda.com`;
    const { data: authData, error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
      email,
      password: data.password,
      options: {
        data: {
          username: data.username,
          display_name: data.display_name,
          user_type: data.user_type,
        }
      }
    });
    if (error) {
      if (error.message.includes('already registered') || error.message.includes('unique')) {
        toast.error('注册失败：用户名已存在');
      } else {
        toast.error('注册失败：' + error.message);
      }
      throw error;
    }

    // signUp 返回但用户未创建（邮箱已存在时 Supabase 返回假成功）
    if (!authData.user) {
      const err = new Error('用户名已被注册，请直接登录或换一个用户名');
      toast.error(err.message);
      throw err;
    }

    // 如果是企业用户，创建企业信息
    if (data.user_type === 'enterprise' && data.company_name && authData.user) {
      await supabase.from('enterprise_profiles').insert({
        profile_id: authData.user.id,
        company_name: data.company_name,
      });
    }

    toast.success('注册成功，欢迎加入！');
  };
```

    if (error) {
      if (error.message.includes('Invalid login credentials') || error.message.includes('invalid_credentials')) {
        toast.error('用户名或密码错误，请重新输入');

      throw error;
    }
    toast.success('登录成功');
